\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01498}01498 \textcolor{comment}{        maximum system call (or maximum API call) interrupt priority.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01499}01499 \textcolor{comment}{        Interrupts that are above the maximum system call priority are keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01500}01500 \textcolor{comment}{        permanently enabled, even when the RTOS kernel is in a critical section,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01501}01501 \textcolor{comment}{        but cannot make any calls to FreeRTOS API functions.  If configASSERT()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01502}01502 \textcolor{comment}{        is defined in FreeRTOSConfig.h then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01503}01503 \textcolor{comment}{        portASSERT\_IF\_INTERRUPT\_PRIORITY\_INVALID() will result in an assertion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01504}01504 \textcolor{comment}{        failure if a FreeRTOS API function is called from an interrupt that has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01505}01505 \textcolor{comment}{        been assigned a priority above the configured maximum system call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01506}01506 \textcolor{comment}{        priority.  Only FreeRTOS functions that end in FromISR can be called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01507}01507 \textcolor{comment}{        from interrupts that have been assigned a priority at or (logically)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01508}01508 \textcolor{comment}{        below the maximum system call interrupt priority.  FreeRTOS maintains a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01509}01509 \textcolor{comment}{        separate interrupt safe API to ensure interrupt entry is as fast and as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01510}01510 \textcolor{comment}{        simple as possible.  More information (albeit Cortex-\/M specific) is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01511}01511 \textcolor{comment}{        provided on the following link:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01512}01512 \textcolor{comment}{        https://www.freertos.org/RTOS-\/Cortex-\/M3-\/M4.html */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01907}01907 \textcolor{comment}{        Interrupts that are above the maximum system call priority are keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01908}01908 \textcolor{comment}{        permanently enabled, even when the RTOS kernel is in a critical section,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01909}01909 \textcolor{comment}{        but cannot make any calls to FreeRTOS API functions.  If configASSERT()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01910}01910 \textcolor{comment}{        is defined in FreeRTOSConfig.h then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01911}01911 \textcolor{comment}{        portASSERT\_IF\_INTERRUPT\_PRIORITY\_INVALID() will result in an assertion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01912}01912 \textcolor{comment}{        failure if a FreeRTOS API function is called from an interrupt that has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01913}01913 \textcolor{comment}{        been assigned a priority above the configured maximum system call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01914}01914 \textcolor{comment}{        priority.  Only FreeRTOS functions that end in FromISR can be called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01915}01915 \textcolor{comment}{        from interrupts that have been assigned a priority at or (logically)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l01916}01916 \textcolor{comment}{        below the maximum system call interrupt priority.  FreeRTOS maintains a}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02303}02303     \textcolor{comment}{/* RTOS ports that support interrupt nesting have the concept of a maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02304}02304 \textcolor{comment}{    system call (or maximum API call) interrupt priority.  Interrupts that are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02305}02305 \textcolor{comment}{    above the maximum system call priority are kept permanently enabled, even}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02306}02306 \textcolor{comment}{    when the RTOS kernel is in a critical section, but cannot make any calls to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02307}02307 \textcolor{comment}{    FreeRTOS API functions.  If configASSERT() is defined in FreeRTOSConfig.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02308}02308 \textcolor{comment}{    then portASSERT\_IF\_INTERRUPT\_PRIORITY\_INVALID() will result in an assertion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02309}02309 \textcolor{comment}{    failure if a FreeRTOS API function is called from an interrupt that has been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02310}02310 \textcolor{comment}{    assigned a priority above the configured maximum system call priority.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02311}02311 \textcolor{comment}{    Only FreeRTOS functions that end in FromISR can be called from interrupts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02312}02312 \textcolor{comment}{    that have been assigned a priority at or (logically) below the maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02313}02313 \textcolor{comment}{    system call interrupt priority.  FreeRTOS maintains a separate interrupt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02314}02314 \textcolor{comment}{    safe API to ensure interrupt entry is as fast and as simple as possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02315}02315 \textcolor{comment}{    More information (albeit Cortex-\/M specific) is provided on the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02316}02316 \textcolor{comment}{    link: https://www.freertos.org/RTOS-\/Cortex-\/M3-\/M4.html */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l02317}02317     \mbox{\hyperlink{_free_r_t_o_s_8h_a10f75d20c71c4289f96d1b89cb6c62e2}{portASSERT\_IF\_INTERRUPT\_PRIORITY\_INVALID}}();}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04321}04321 \textcolor{comment}{         *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04327}04327 \textcolor{comment}{         * might bloat the code size, use a lot of stack, and provide different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04328}04328 \textcolor{comment}{         * results on different platforms.  An alternative, tiny, third party,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04329}04329 \textcolor{comment}{         * and limited functionality implementation of sprintf() is provided in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04330}04330 \textcolor{comment}{         * many of the FreeRTOS/Demo sub-\/directories in a file called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04331}04331 \textcolor{comment}{         * printf-\/stdarg.c (note printf-\/stdarg.c does not provide a full}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04333}04333 \textcolor{comment}{         *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04334}04334 \textcolor{comment}{         * It is recommended that production systems call uxTaskGetSystemState()}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04427}04427 \textcolor{comment}{         * vTaskGetRunTimeStats() calls uxTaskGetSystemState(), then formats part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04428}04428 \textcolor{comment}{         * of the uxTaskGetSystemState() output into a human readable table that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04429}04429 \textcolor{comment}{         * displays the amount of time each task has spent in the Running state}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04433}04433 \textcolor{comment}{         * function that might bloat the code size, use a lot of stack, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04434}04434 \textcolor{comment}{         * provide different results on different platforms.  An alternative,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04435}04435 \textcolor{comment}{         * tiny, third party, and limited functionality implementation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04436}04436 \textcolor{comment}{         * sprintf() is provided in many of the FreeRTOS/Demo sub-\/directories in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04437}04437 \textcolor{comment}{         * a file called printf-\/stdarg.c (note printf-\/stdarg.c does not provide}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04439}04439 \textcolor{comment}{         *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04440}04440 \textcolor{comment}{         * It is recommended that production systems call uxTaskGetSystemState()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04441}04441 \textcolor{comment}{         * directly to get access to raw stats data, rather than indirectly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04442}04442 \textcolor{comment}{         * through a call to vTaskGetRunTimeStats().}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04837}04837         \textcolor{comment}{/* RTOS ports that support interrupt nesting have the concept of a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04838}04838 \textcolor{comment}{        maximum system call (or maximum API call) interrupt priority.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04839}04839 \textcolor{comment}{        Interrupts that are above the maximum system call priority are keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04840}04840 \textcolor{comment}{        permanently enabled, even when the RTOS kernel is in a critical section,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tasks_8c_source_l04841}04841 \textcolor{comment}{        but cannot make any calls to FreeRTOS API functions.  If configASSERT()}}
